  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>

  <td width="46%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:46.22%;">

  </td>

  <td width="46%" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:46.22%;">

  </td>
  <td width="47%" colspan="2" valign="top" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:47.28%;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">STEWART &amp; STEVENSON SERVICES REPORTS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SECOND QUARTER 2004 RESULTS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter Net Earnings were $0.20 per
Diluted Share</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Net Earnings from Continuing Operations were
$0.25 per Diluted Share</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">HOUSTON &#150;
August 25, 2004 &#150; Stewart &amp; Stevenson Services, Inc. (NYSE: SVC) announced
results for the second quarter of fiscal 2004, which ended on July 31, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales for the
second quarter of fiscal 2004 totaled $316.3 million compared to sales of
$312.9 million recorded in the same period a year ago.&#160; Net earnings in the second quarter of fiscal
2004 were $5.9 million or $0.20 per diluted share compared to $0.11 per diluted
share in the second quarter of fiscal 2003.&#160;
Included in this result was a loss of $1.4 million or $0.05 per diluted
share from discontinued operations related to adjustments to liabilities recorded
for obligations from the company&#146;s blowout preventer, valve, elastomer, and
drilling riser business which was sold during fiscal 2002.&#160; Net earnings from continuing operations in
the second quarter of fiscal 2004 were $7.3 million or $0.25 per diluted share
compared to $3.2 million or $0.11 per diluted share in the second quarter of
fiscal 2003.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Max L. Lukens,
the company&#146;s President and Chief Executive Officer, stated, &#147;We are encouraged
by these results as they reflect the benefits of the strategic actions we have
implemented to generate acceptable returns in our core businesses and to
position Stewart &amp; Stevenson for sustained profitable growth.&#160; While we are pleased with the improved
results, we intend to build upon this progress, and we are committed to taking
the actions required to achieve our desired level of returns.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Segment Data</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">Tactical Vehicle Systems</font></u>  </b>segment, which
manufactures tactical vehicles for the U.S. Army and others, recorded sales of
$140.7 million in the second quarter of fiscal 2004 compared to $108.4 million
in the prior year&#146;s second quarter.&#160;
Operating profit for the second quarter of fiscal 2004 improved to $18.8
million compared to $17.3 million in the second quarter of fiscal 2003
primarily as a result of the higher sales volume.&#160; Operating margin percentages were lower in
fiscal 2004 as a result of higher material costs, primarily related to
increased steel pricing, and product mix.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company&#146;s
current multi-year contract with the U.S. Army to produce the Family of Medium
Tactical Vehicles (&#147;FMTV&#148;) is scheduled to conclude during the second half of
fiscal 2004 at which time production is expected to begin under the new
multi-year FMTV contract.&#160; The <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">Power Products</font></u></b> segment, which is
responsible for sales and aftermarket support of a wide range of industrial and
transportation equipment, recorded sales of $123.7 million in the second
quarter compared to sales of $127.9 million a year ago.&#160; Sales in fiscal 2004 were lower primarily as
a result of the exit of certain product lines.&#160;
The second quarter 2004 operating profit totaled $1.8 million compared
to a $5.6 million operating loss in the comparable period of fiscal 2003.&#160; The improved results are largely attributable
to the numerous ongoing actions taken beginning in the second half of 2003
aimed at improving the quality of sales and reducing operating costs.&#160; These actions include reductions in the
workforce, closure of facilities, and the exit of certain product lines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">Engineered Products</font></u>  </b>segment<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">, </font></b>which manufactures equipment for the well
servicing industry, as well as mobile railcar movers, off-road seismic
vehicles, and snow blowers, recorded sales of$21.9 million for the second quarter of fiscal 2004 compared to
$38.3 million in the same quarter last year.&#160;
Sales for the second quarter of fiscal 2003 included a higher volume of
international well servicing equipment orders that were completed during the
second half of the year.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\mbrandt\04-9948-1\task177164\9948-1-mm.htm',USER='mbrandt',CD='Aug 24 21:24 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Operating profit for the second quarter of fiscal 2004 increased to
$1.1 million compared to $0.6 million in the previous year and included a $0.6
million gain from the sale of an idle manufacturing facility.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">Distributed Energy Solutions</font></u></b> segment
recorded second quarter 2004 sales of $6.2 million compared to sales of $20.0
million in the same period of fiscal 2003.&#160;
Second quarter 2004 operating loss totaled $5.8 million compared to a
$2.8 million loss in the comparable period of last year primarily as a result
of lower sales volume and ongoing indirect expenses as well as costs associated
with the execution of the remaining contractual obligations in this segment and
various contract issues and disputes. As previously announced, the company has
decided to exit the turnkey engineering, procurement, and construction (&#147;EPC&#148;)
activities of this segment and continues to wind up the remaining contractual
obligations associated with such activity.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b><u><font style="font-weight:bold;">Airline Products</font></u></b> segment, which
manufactures aviation ground support products, recorded sales of $23.7 million
in the second quarter of fiscal 2004 compared to $18.4 million in the same
quarter last year.&#160; Operating loss for
the second quarter of 2004 was $0.6 million compared to a $0.7 million loss in
the corresponding period of fiscal 2003.&#160;
The increased sales volume was partially offset by higher material
costs, primarily related to increased steel prices, higher operating expenses,
and unfavorable product mix.&#160;&#160; As
previously announced, the company is pursuing a possible sale of its Airline
Products business.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Liquidity</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total cash and
short-term investments were $99.8 million at July 31, 2004 as compared to
$106.3 million at the end of the first quarter.&#160;
Net cash used in operating activities during the second quarter was $9.7
million and included a $32 million impact from decreases in progress payments
related to the transition to the new U.S. Army contract at TVS.&#160; Net cash provided by investing activities was
$5.5 million and included $11.4 million of proceeds from the sale of certain
rental equipment assets and two idle manufacturing facilities.&#160; Financing activities consumed $2.0 million of
cash primarily related to the regularly scheduled quarterly dividend payment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Stewart &amp; Stevenson Services has
scheduled a conference call for Wednesday, August 25, 2004 at 10:00 a.m.
Eastern Time to review second quarter results.&#160;
To listen to the call, dial 800-659-1966 or 617-614-2711 and use pass
code 80041855 at least ten minutes before the conference call begins.&#160; A telephonic replay of the conference call
will be available through September 1, 2004 and may be accessed by dialing
888-286-8010 or 617-801-6888 and using pass code 48720311.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investors, analysts, and the general public
will also have the opportunity to listen to the conference call free over the
Internet by visiting the company&#146;s web site at www.ssss.com.&#160; To listen to the live call on the web, please
visit the Stewart &amp; Stevenson web site at least fifteen minutes early to
register, download, and install any necessary audio software.&#160; For those who cannot listen to the live web
cast, an audio archive will be available shortly after the call ends.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Stewart &amp;
Stevenson Services, Inc., founded in 1902, is a billion-dollar company that
manufactures, distributes, and provides service for a wide range of industrial
products and diesel-powered equipment to key industries worldwide, including
power generation, defense, airline, marine, petroleum, and transportation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>
